const BASE = { responsive: true, plugins: { legend: { labels: { color: '#8b8fa8', font: { size: 11 } } } } };

// 1. Category bar
new Chart('categoryChart', {
  type: 'bar',
  data: {
    labels: CAT_DATA.labels,
    datasets: [{ data: CAT_DATA.values, backgroundColor: P, borderRadius: 6, borderSkipped: false }]
  },
  options: { ...BASE, indexAxis: 'y',
    plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
    scales: { x: { grid: { color: '#1e2030' }, ticks: { color: '#8b8fa8' } },
               y: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { color: '#c8cadf', font: { size: 11 } } } }
  }
});

// 2. Fan-out doughnut
new Chart('fanOutChart', {
  type: 'doughnut',
  data: {
    labels: FO_DATA.labels,
    datasets: [{ data: FO_DATA.values, backgroundColor: P, borderWidth: 2, borderColor: '#1a1d27', hoverOffset: 8 }]
  },
  options: { ...BASE, cutout: '58%',
    plugins: { legend: { position: 'right', labels: { color: '#8b8fa8', padding: 10, font: { size: 11 } } } }
  }
});

// 3. User type bar (rules applicable per user type)
new Chart('userTypeChart', {
  type: 'bar',
  data: {
    labels: UT_DATA.labels,
    datasets: [{ data: UT_DATA.values, backgroundColor: P, borderRadius: 6 }]
  },
  options: { ...BASE, indexAxis: 'y',
    plugins: { legend: { display: false },
      tooltip: { callbacks: { label: ctx => ` ${ctx.raw.toLocaleString()} rule applications` } } },
    scales: { x: { grid: { color: '#1e2030' }, ticks: { color: '#8b8fa8' } },
               y: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { color: '#c8cadf', font: { size: 11 } } } }
  }
});

// 4. Monthly trend
new Chart('trendChart', {
  type: 'line',
  data: {
    labels: TR_DATA.labels,
    datasets: [{
      label: 'Rules Created', data: TR_DATA.values,
      borderColor: '#6c63ff', backgroundColor: 'rgba(108,99,255,0.1)',
      borderWidth: 2, fill: true, tension: 0.4, pointRadius: 3, pointHoverRadius: 6, pointBackgroundColor: '#6c63ff'
    }]
  },
  options: { ...BASE,
    plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
    scales: {
      x: { grid: { color: '#1e2030' }, ticks: { color: '#8b8fa8', maxRotation: 45,
            callback: function(val, idx) { return idx % 3 === 0 ? TR_DATA.labels[idx] : ''; } } },
      y: { grid: { color: '#1e2030' }, ticks: { color: '#8b8fa8' } }
    }
  }
});

// 5. Top rule types
new Chart('ruleTypeChart', {
  type: 'bar',
  data: {
    labels: RT_DATA.labels.map(l => l.length > 22 ? l.substring(0,22)+'…' : l),
    datasets: [{ data: RT_DATA.values, backgroundColor: P.concat(P).slice(0, RT_DATA.values.length), borderRadius: 5 }]
  },
  options: { ...BASE, indexAxis: 'y',
    plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
    scales: { x: { grid: { color: '#1e2030' }, ticks: { color: '#8b8fa8' } },
               y: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { color: '#c8cadf', font: { size: 10 } } } }
  }
});

// 6. Countries
new Chart('countryChart', {
  type: 'bar',
  data: {
    labels: CC_DATA.labels,
    datasets: [{ data: CC_DATA.values,
      backgroundColor: CC_DATA.labels.map((_, i) => `hsl(${220 + i * 5}, 70%, ${55 + (i % 4) * 5}%)`),
      borderRadius: 5 }]
  },
  options: { ...BASE,
    plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
    scales: { x: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { color: '#8b8fa8', font: { size: 11 } } },
               y: { grid: { color: '#1e2030' }, ticks: { color: '#8b8fa8' } } }
  }
});

// 7. Migration stacked bar
new Chart('migrationChart', {
  type: 'bar',
  data: {
    labels: MIG_CAT.labels.map(l => l.length > 20 ? l.substring(0,20)+'…' : l),
    datasets: [
      { label: 'Migrated ✅', data: MIG_CAT.migrated, backgroundColor: '#00d4aa', borderRadius: 4 },
      { label: 'Not Migrated ⏳', data: MIG_CAT.not_migrated, backgroundColor: '#ff6b6b', borderRadius: 4 }
    ]
  },
  options: { ...BASE, indexAxis: 'y',
    scales: { x: { stacked: true, grid: { color: '#1e2030' }, ticks: { color: '#8b8fa8' } },
               y: { stacked: true, grid: { display: false }, ticks: { color: '#c8cadf', font: { size: 11 } } } },
    plugins: { legend: { labels: { color: '#8b8fa8', font: { size: 11 } } } }
  }
});

// 8. Migration % bar
new Chart('migPctChart', {
  type: 'bar',
  data: {
    labels: MIG_PCT.labels.map(l => l.length > 22 ? l.substring(0,22)+'…' : l),
    datasets: [{
      label: '% Migrated',
      data: MIG_PCT.values,
      backgroundColor: MIG_PCT.values.map(v => v === 100 ? '#00d4aa' : v === 0 ? '#ff6b6b' : v > 60 ? '#6c63ff' : '#ffd166'),
      borderRadius: 6
    }]
  },
  options: { ...BASE, indexAxis: 'y',
    plugins: { legend: { display: false },
      tooltip: { callbacks: { label: ctx => ` ${ctx.raw}% migrated` } } },
    scales: {
      x: { grid: { color: '#1e2030' }, ticks: { color: '#8b8fa8', callback: v => v+'%' }, max: 100 },
      y: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { color: '#c8cadf', font: { size: 11 } } }
    }
  }
});

// === TABLE ===
const utPills = {
  'Employee': 'pill-blue', 'Client': 'pill-orange', 'DirectEmployee': 'pill-teal',
  'HRISDirectEmployee': 'pill-yellow', 'Contractor': 'pill-red', 'PEOEmployee': 'pill-grey'
};
const catPills = {
  'EOR': 'pill-teal', 'GP (Global Payroll)': 'pill-blue', 'Compliance & Checks': 'pill-orange',
  'Payroll & Tax': 'pill-green', 'Contracts': 'pill-yellow', 'Expenses': 'pill-red',
  'Offboarding / Termination': 'pill-grey', 'Time & Scheduling': 'pill-blue', 'Other': 'pill-grey'
};

function renderTable(rules) {
  const display = rules.slice(0, 500);
  document.getElementById('tableBody').innerHTML = display.map(r => {
    const pCat = catPills[r.CATEGORY] || 'pill-grey';
    const pUt  = utPills[r.USER_TYPE] || 'pill-grey';
    const pMig = r.IS_MIGRATED_TO_ENGINE === 'Yes' ? 'pill-green' : 'pill-red';
    const utCount = r.user_type_count > 1 
      ? `<span class="pill pill-yellow" title="Applies to ${r.user_type_count} user types">${r.user_type_count} types</span>` 
      : `<span class="pill pill-grey">1 type</span>`;
    return `<tr>
      <td><span class="rule-name" title="${r.RULE_NAME}">${r.RULE_NAME || '—'}</span></td>
      <td style="color:#8b8fa8;font-size:11.5px;max-width:180px;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">${r.RULE_TYPE || '—'}</td>
      <td><span class="pill ${pCat}">${r.CATEGORY || '—'}</span></td>
      <td style="font-weight:600;color:#c8cadf;">${r.COUNTRY_CODE || '—'}</td>
      <td style="color:#8b8fa8;">${r.CURRENCY || '—'}</td>
      <td><span class="pill ${pUt}">${r.USER_TYPE || '—'}</span></td>
      <td>${utCount}</td>
      <td><span class="pill ${pMig}">${{'Yes':'✅ Yes','No':'⏳ No'}[r.IS_MIGRATED_TO_ENGINE] || '—'}</span></td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');
  document.getElementById('rowCountBadge').textContent = rules.length.toLocaleString() + ' unique rules';
  document.getElementById('tableCount').textContent = 
    `Showing ${Math.min(500, rules.length).toLocaleString()} of ${rules.length.toLocaleString()} matching rules`;
}

function applyFilters() {
  const q  = document.getElementById('searchInput').value.toLowerCase();
  const cat = document.getElementById('catFilter').value;
  const ut  = document.getElementById('userFilter').value;
  const mig = document.getElementById('migFilter').value;
  const filtered = ALL_RULES.filter(r => {
    if (q && ![(r.RULE_NAME||''),(r.RULE_TYPE||''),(r.COUNTRY_CODE||''),(r.CATEGORY||''),(r.CURRENCY||'')]
              .some(s => s.toLowerCase().includes(q))) return false;
    if (cat && r.CATEGORY !== cat) return false;
    if (ut  && r.USER_TYPE !== ut) return false;
    if (mig && r.IS_MIGRATED_TO_ENGINE !== mig) return false;
    return true;
  });
  renderTable(filtered);
}

['searchInput','catFilter','userFilter','migFilter'].forEach(id =>
  document.getElementById(id).addEventListener(id === 'searchInput' ? 'input' : 'change', applyFilters)
);

renderTable(ALL_RULES);
</script>
</body>
</html>
